UNSINGIZI KASANGWENI. 

Ukufa kukanina, uThembckilc, umkaSangwcni Nifundile enewadini kaGongoda ngoNsingizi, uma sen ikhohliwe, akenithi ngqabithi keniyokuthi yaphalazi nje khona kuyo. 

    Phela into ayeyifela wubusoka bakhe, lobu obufelwayo nanamuhla lokhu ngikhuluma nje. Nangaphandle k\\aloyamuzi owaehithekayo, ngoba insizwa yakhona yafunyanwa izothakatha cbusuku, isizoqedela kuNsingizi, yabanjwa zintelezi zikaBhengu, ngoba wayeyemuke intombi, kodwa kwakungewlIwo wodwa umuzi owawuzonda uNsingizi, kodwa yayiminingi impela. Wayezondwa zinsinzwa eziningi ezazifuna ukumehoboza ngamalumbo, ezinye ezingafuni ukukhunkula, zifuna ukumbhambabula ngenqayi. Kukhona namakhosikazi emizi yawo ayembuka amnyonkoloze uNsingizi, edlule ashingizele nje kuye engambingeleli, ngoba ezondela abantwana bawo abaWuphayo ngokubamisa kabi ezintombini, nasezeshelini zabo. Kwamenza ukuba angabe esaphuza kweminye imizi yangakubo, eseyikhetha angaphuza kuyo. Noyise naye wayeseyame njalo ukumnqanda ekusabalaleni ethi kaziqoqe mpela, uhamba phezu kwewa ku.,esiphepho esingahie simholokodisele kulo. 

    PhD, wayebonisa ubani, uNsingizi wayengu-angikhathali nje. Waqhubeka nobusoka bakhe, kodwa waziqoqa akasahalala ematshv..aleni, nasemizini yabantu. 

    Hhayi-ke wayesephilile uNsingizi, esebuyele ebunsimeni bakhe eseyisisasadolo ngiyakutshela bo, sensizwa, emya kokuyuka kwakhe eeansini lokufa; nogazi lwakhe luyilokhu lumi luthe phuhle. Izinsizwa zangakubo zamzonda, zifuna ambathe inhlabathi; kodwa zazingezame, noma zimlokothe nje ngenqayi; ngoba zazingabe ziziehome kwamalunda. Ngamakhambi zazingabe zidlala ngegeja kuziliwe. Nokho-ke zake zazama ngakho kokubili, zashaya phansi okwendlala yanyakenye; ngoba lwalumelaphile ukhukhumba lakwaBhengu. 

    Nokho-ke wabona uSangweni ukuba qha! amanqe ayamzulela umtanakhe; angaze amudle; kuhle akagudluke kaneane kulesosifunda saphezu kwePhondwane elineane 



 

ake ayofuna inkonzo kwezinye izifunda, mhlayimbe angake ahlale azinze, adIe kwehle nokudla; akalale behle nobuthongo Jobu bambala. 

    Wahlanganisa umuzi wakhc ewuchazela ukuba akusendawo ebafaneleyo lena abakuyo, ngoba bahlezi phezll kwameva. Pho-ke uma ameva elokhu umuntu emhlaba njalo ewabangula kodwa, isigcino uze ahlatshwe yisiqopholozi seva sephukele phakathi, kubelukhuni ukulibanguJa. 

    Vmuzi wakhe wathi ukhuluma izwi lempela. Nango-ke eIibhedula izwe uSangweni eya kwaSincinta, lapho kwakhe khona umnakwabo uMaIiwa waseLangeni, okwakunguyena ndunankuIu yesigodi sakwaSincinta; eyofuna inkonzo khona. 

    Lathi lapho Iithi chasha nje, wayezithintitha uSangweni, esebuhlambile ubuso nezandla; wetshatha ijazi lakhe lesisosha ehlombe; ethatha umshiza wakhe wcphahla, nomphondi wegqeba, eminya umcakulwana wesitshodwana sotshwala, evafelisa emzini wakhe, ethi nxa kuze kupheJe amasuku amane-mahlanu, bangabimehlwana nxa bengamboni; ngoba njengomuntu osewaxhwala, woke ahlabe ikhefu kwaMnakwabo uMaJiwa. 

    Nanguya-ke uSangweni elimbulula eqonde kwaSincinta; ethi eyakuthi memfu nje, kwaMbatha, emzini kaSihosho uyise kaBikwaphi noNtombikayise selifudumele Banga impela. Ame ngaphandle kothango engangeni; ethi angabambeka nxa engangena. Bambingelele khona ngaphandJe abaseMambatheni; bethi aze ab.khonzele kuNtombikayise, nakuMaliwa. 

    Behlukane-ke ngoba ufuna ukufika kusakhanya kwaSineinta uSangweni, ngoba akawazi ngokusobala umnzi wakoMaliwa. 

    Washaya ngapha kudanyana nomnzi kaMalombo waseLangeni, umfowabo kaMaliwa, uSangweni, eyowela uMkhuze, eyowela iSihJenga, eyowela uManzawayo noCansane, kwakuqundeka amehlo-ke, ngaleyo nkathi, kwazise ukuthi nokho abantu basebemkhombisile ukuthi umuphi umuzi womna. kwabo uMaliwa. Khona-ke wafika kuhwalele kuphelele nya. Wathi Iapho emaqondana nesango, waquzwa yizinja, abafana bazikhuza; bamngenisa kwamnumzane uMaliwa.

UKULAHLEKA NOKUFUNYANWA KUKAMAHLATHINI 

Kwavela umhlolo obungalindelwe kaMapbaphu. 

    Akubanga nkathi ende, uNsingizi bascmi namfazi Iowa, khona uNsingizi wayesevalelisa engena indlela; amabombo ewaqondisa ngakubo. Watika kuqundeka amehlo ekhaya, edlula ngakubo kaGongoda kuqala, emfumana emi engame isibaya; abafana besenga, 

"'Uhambe kanjani na kanina?" Kubuza uGongoda. "Ngihambe kabanyana kaaina mpela." Amxoxelc ukuba uhambo Iwakhe lubelubi ngayiphi indlela. 

    "Hawn uyazi njena kanina, ngikhohlwe ukukutshela ukuba kuyo yona leyomizi oyishoyo, kunomuzi wasckhakonyoko kwaSibiya; ngoba phela wawakhe la, wathutha-ke waya kulo leliya IakwaButhelezi. UBhengu-ke yena ungale kwaleziyantaba ozibonile njalo zithi lokoloko; ngoba libanzi phela izwe leliya lakwaButhelezi." 

    Hayi-ke uNsingizi aye kubo naye; amxoxele uyisc ngohambo Iwakhe, nezinkathazo ezingapho kwclakwaButltelezi; nokuthi naye sibili uyatisa ukuyofuna, ngoba kukhona kuyo leyomizi ekhakonina; utshelwe nguGongoda; uzofikela khona adimane elala khona. 

    Phela naye uSangweni wayesazi ukuthi ebukhweni bakhe sekwaba kulo lelo lakwaButhelezi, indawo nje ayengazi ukuba ikuphi. Wamvulela uyise ukuba ahambe ayohlwaya, ngoba nangu uyambona uyashiseka. 

    Nango-ke evuka ngoviv! eluvathuza futhi uhambo Iwakhe Iwangayizolo; ethi enhliziyweni yakhe mhlayimbe, use tholakele nje umfunwa. Wadabula lelohlathi leNgome elesabekayo, wayeyibona leyandawo lapho ebemi khona naleya ntombi yangayizolo, naloya mfazi othe wendele kwaNdlela. 

    Wehla waqonda kuyo leyomizi, eyofuna kuqala umuzi wasekhakonina. Wafika emuzini wokuqala awawunamathele emginqilizini; eduze kwawo kunomtapo wensoyi. Wakhangwa yingqashumba lekhehla, limi eceleni kwesithole esinkone, sinomvemve, sisandakuwulahla phansi nje. Sekuyindadavu nje yekhehla.

    K wakuyindawo yabathakathi, incane, njengoba sengike ngathi fahlafahla ngaphambidlana. Umphakathi wayo wawusithwe zinguzungu zamatshe; ngaphez.ulu kuyisiwana. KWAHLANGANA UNOKUHLEKA NOHLEKISILE. 

Igazi Iiyezwana ngikutshele. 

     OmzakaNsingi7i (ababili), ngakusasa ehambe ngayizolo uNsingizi yena,. bahlangana noNokuhleka, evela emfnleni kade eyokha amanzi, Iapho bamtshela ukuthi ubekhona uNsingizi kodwa ubehambe ngomcimbi, yikho ehambe engasavelanga nangakuyc nje. kodwa uzoshesha abuye futhi eze ngapho masinyane. 

     Wathi ukumoyizela kanoane uNokuhleka ebheka eerleni. aze akapakelwe ngamanzi ebusweni, wathi, "Ha, ningitshcla leyondaba yalowo mfoka7i, nginandabani naye'! Uyisoka lami yini?      Athi uNokuhleka, "Qha-ke. Sibiya, akudikizi naneele, angazi nokuthi bekufikeni yani. Salani kahle-ke." Asho ethi ukukhweza amathundu ehamba.

KW APIQIKA AMANYALA MA YEBABO!! 

UMaliwa uyofaka udaba kuMutwana. 

WAKHULUMA WAQOTHULA KUMNTWANA UGONGODA. 

     Phela uMntwana wayewathumile amadoda, ukuba ayotshela uSangweni ukuthi indodana yakhe isibulele umuntu. Pho-ke yena ubethe izinsizwa ebezilapho naya, azimyise kwagoqanyawo; kodwa yadlubulundela. Akazi-ke ukuthi ishonephi; kodwa uyayifuna ukuba nayo ife njengomfo wakwaGodloza embulole. Wamemezela uMntwana. ukuba oyombona uNsingi7i Iowa, angemethusi, kodwa azohlehela yena, khona yena eyomthumela ngezinsizloVa ziyomhanqa, zimbambe zimbulale naye, njeng0ba chulelc naye. 

     Uyisc kaNsingizi-ke, uSangweni, wathi kanalizwi angalisho, nxa umntanakhe enze amanyala anjalo. Wathi akukho okungumbono, nokuyisenzo sakhe uMntwana angakuphikisa yenaSangweni; konke nje kodwa akushilo kulungile. 

     Wathi engewatshwa-ke uMaweni, insizwa kaNkabinde, ngakusasa, ayesefikile amadoda ayethunywe nguMnl wana kuSangweni. aze adlula cyobikcla noMaliwa uNdunankulu wakhe uMntwana; owaphendula wathi yena; "\Vewu, wakwenza okukhulu umntanomnakwethu. Ingabe umbulaleleni umfana kaNsibankulu; bebexabene ngani naye. Kodwa isizathu sosizwa; azihambi phallsi." 
Wayesefunwc-ke kwadelwa ukuba akasekho uNsingizi. 
UGongoda waycscfunc waze wazimela naye kuzo zonke izindawo acabangela kuza, njengoba umfana wakwaboNsingizi efika nodaba kuy' lokuthi usekhona usawadln amabele uNsingizi. Akazange ahlebele ngisho oyedwa uGongoda wakubo ngaJoludaba. ngisho onina imbala. 

     Kuthc-ke nxa uMdelwa noMziwenduku noGongoda hcthi kuSangweni kayomangala enduneni enkulu uMaliwa, kwamuma nje uSangwcni ukuthi uzomangala athini. Kodwa babanaye oMdelwa noMziwenduku nxa emangala bemelekelela ngczimpendulo namazwi okumangala "qobo.

WAGULA-KE UNSINGIZI BAKITHI. 

    Kwase kuqalainyanga kaNhlolanja ngemuva kwalandela eyoMkhosi nxa sekuphele izinsuku ezisiphohlongo etholakala uNsingizi, lapho kwalungiselelwa umgeageo kadadewabo kaNsingizi, oyinkosazana kaSangweni; lapho kwahlabeka uNsingizi kabana, ebholokoqa inyongo engapheli; ehanjiswa nayisisu scgazi; konke Iokho kwachitha amalungiselelo omgcageo, abantu baze bafakana imilomo bethi, "Kuyala yini kanti ukuba code umtakaSangweni; sinyama sini lesi csisendlelclli yakhe." 
    K walandwa uBhengu ukuba azokwcnza izaba; kod\va yena uqobo wafunyanwa ebangwa ncgodi, engenamandla nawokuthi nyaka. Baze balanda eyayikhona khona kwaSineinta, leya eyake yamphathaphatha uNsingizi. Yafike nokho inyanga y;:tlinqanda igazi. nokuhlanza inyongo eluhlaza, kodwa kwaqhuma cbomvu eyiqanda.     Wabuye waphila okaSangweni, kungakabi kude kakhulu, wonda kodwa. wabangamathambo; wabuyc wancwatshana. 

    Kuthc ngelinye ilanga, wake wathatha izagile zakhc. wabiza izinja. wake wayozingela. Wahlwaya, wahlwaya. ngisho kekuvuke ngisho unogwaja yedwa lona. Wabuya-ke uNsingizi; waHka cdllze Ilempophoma wahlala phansi kwcsihlahla esasinomkhulu t:mthunzi. csaphumula. 

    Wafikclwa ngllmfanekiso emqondweni \vakhe, kadadcwabo kaMdelwa iseshcli sakhe, noJahulilc wakwaZulu. 

    Wafikelwa yisihlwathi; wathi esathc loka nje, waphupha intombi angayaziyo, enhlc isclawini lakhe; kodwa ilawu lakhe licitshwe ngcmikhonto ithc vekelele nje. WABANJWA KANJANI UNSINGIZI? 

    Mhla efikayo kwelakwaButhelezi nje, uNsingizi, eya ekhakonina, kadwa eqonde ukuyabona isishcli sakhe, yambona enye yezinsizwa zakoSifile; yayawuhlaba umkhosi ukuthi nangu uNsingizi engapha kulesisifunda sakwaButhelezi. 
Waqazwa ukubonwa nxa cschamba, zinsizwa zakoSifilc. 

Zambona eya ensimini, lapho kulinda khona udadewaba kaMdclwa; nanxa esebllya; zabona ukuthi uyalala. Zavilka ekuseni ngakusasa zayoqaza, zambona eya futhi ensimini abekuyo ngayizolo; nanxa esebuya; nanxa escsuka ekhakonina esehamba eya kubo uNsingizi, zambona; zagijirna zayomlalela ehlathini laseNgome, zihuqana ebusweni nasemzimbcni ngentshede, ezaziyiphethe zithi; "Khana lingekusibona iqili leliya, ngoba funa lidlubulundele, Iibaleke, kanti selisibanile ukuthi singobani; liseneke kakhulu." 
    Ihlathi leNgome lana, lalilibi ngisho emini nje, lesabeka. licinene, linesisinda; umuntu aze aphume kulo. kadc bani kuqine umzimba ukuba usephumile ngcmpela. 

    Umuzi kaSifile. wawulokhu umsongele uNsingizi, ngokuyovumbulula uMaphaphu, noMahlathini Ie, csiweni sabo, esachitheka ngenxa yakhe naso. benoMdclwa, noMziwempi. 

    Babefunga begomela, bethi noma bengamtholanga esaphila, bayomumba elibeni lakhe, ngisho esengamathambo bayokhunkula ngaye, benaye uMdelwa naMziwenduku njalo. 

    USifile nomuzi wonke wakhe, wayengumthakathi, ethakatha impela; lIkuthakatha kwakhe sekwaze kwamehlukanisa nomfowabo, owayeyiwcle naye. waya kwakha yedwa klldanyana, ethi uyasiphoxa singamaShcnge umfowethu ngokuthakatha, singathakathi thina maShenge. zasezimhcha izingozi, zixabhelela imbangi yazo uNsingizi zithi ubulewe yiyo uMaweni, kanti yizo izitha zakhe uNsingizi ezimbulelc. WAPHATHA KAHLE ABANTU UGONGODA. 

Indinyana yokugcina kulencwadi. 

     Yisiqephu sokugcina lesi kulencwadi enginilobelc yona. cbizwa ngokuthiwa, NGU-NSINGIZJ. Niyokhumbula ukuba lena ilandela engaqala ngayo UGONGODA. Nalena-ke yesibili enhloko yenkulumo yayo inguNsingizi, nezinhlupheko, nezinkathazo zakhe esenizifundile nazizwa, nazizwisisa, ngiyiphetha ngaye umnikaziyo.ke uGongoda, umuntu ngomqwayiba; insizwa ngenkani; umfo kaMali",a Mhlongo, njengoba eyokuqala nayo isuke ngaye; nanxa kungasekho lutho engizolusho ngomkakhe uNtombikayise owase engumkakhe escmganile kulenkathi. 

Senizwile-ke nokuthi uNdunankulu, uMaliwa uyise kaGongoda wagcina ngokubhubha njengoba wayescmpilwana ediniwe. Uthi-ke nxa esehamba elizweni uMaliwa, "Mnta~ nami, Gongoda, njcngDba, sengiya ekuphumuleni nje, ukhumbule ukuba umsebenzi nesikhundla sami sizosala siwela en;ahlombe akho. Pho-ke mntanami ngiyakwazi, ungowami, ukuba uyixhamaxhama leshinga lokulwa, kodwa kuzodingeka manjc ubeyishinga lokukhuluma, lokweJamula abantu. Um~ shiza lana, klizofuneka uwuhlome ezintungweni llwethule uma uyobulala inyoka. Kubantu umshiza wakho kubengumlorno narnazwi agatha. Nxa wenze njengoba ngikulaya uyobaphatha abantu lIze ukhokhobc. Umuntll ophethe abantu ubalivaka lokulwa. nelokubathuka imbala, angaxhamazeJeli ukulwa nokushaya, kodwa abemnene; abenengalo elinganayo kubo bonke abaphetheyo. Ngiyazi awabekwa kuwe amabili ngenye insizwa, kodwa namuhla nje azobekwa abezi~ nkulungwanc; kodwa onke uwathele ngabandayo. Uzobayinsika yalesisifunda, kodwa ungalibali ukuthi insika yinto enkulu endlini, kodwa uyofumana abachobF izintwala beziehobela khona ku~o namazeze, nezimbungulll imbala kodwa izithulcle nje, Nawe bazochobela kuwe zonke izinto Jezi abazithanda}o uzithulele nje." ISANCAPHE SALENCW ADJ. 

Mhlayimbe funa ungasizwa isihloko salesi siqeshana. 
Kodwa abangabakwaZulu, nabakebalunguza kwadeda-ngendlale, isancaphe bayasazi. 
    Nxa sekulinywe kwaqedwa kuleliya JakwaZulu, kuba nezivanjana zombila abavama ukuvalelisa ngazo abangesibo ovilavoco. Lczi zivanjana kuthi umbila namabele sekomile, zona zibeziseluhlaza, zifulwa kuphekwa ifutho njengasehlobo; igama laza kuthiwa izancaphe. Senizwilc-ke ukuba isancaphe siyini, nokuthi sisho ukuthini-ke kulencwadi. kulesi siqeshana. Sengizothathela ngelide-ke ijubane, ngiye phambili, ngithathele ngihambe nginguntula kodwa. 
    Nizwile kulencwadi ukuthi lapho ayelelc khona cbuya ekuzingeleni uNsingizi, emva kwecala lakhe elalimenze ahlale eTome njengesilwane, waphupha intombi enhle iselawini lakhe, kodwa ilawu lelo licitshwe ngemikhonto. Lokho kwaku yisiboniso sokuthi leyontombi enhle, nguNomfula; kodwa ezomthola ngokuhlangana naye ekuhluphekeni, nasezingozini zokufa. Njengoba nempela batholana bavumana esiwcni sosizi lokufa, nxa umphefumlo kaNsingizi wawulcng~la cgcbeni lethuna elingafani namanye amathuna abonwayo, kodwa elakhe okwakufanele kubekuyilokhu kuthiwa, "Ingabe wenze njani; ingabe wadliwa yini; ingabe usaphila noma sewafa yini." 
    Lesiya sihlahla, abambamba uNsingizi, bambophcla kuso ngentambo, ehlathini leNgome. bengakamyisi esiweni sabathakathi, akuyikho ukuba abathakathi babcbabophela kuso njalo ababanjwa babo; bambophela nje uNsingizi kuso ngoba kuyisihlahla abafana bakaSilile, bembophela ngoqhotho ababeluphethe, bezingela bcluphethe, kodwa beluphathele khona ukumbopha ngalo uNsingizi nxa bemtholiIe. Lesosihlahla sasingafani nalesiya sasesiweni esincane, okwakuboshelwe kuso uMahlathini, sona okwakungumscbenzi waso ukuba kuboshelwe kuso abantu ababanjiwe, sinezintambo zaso-izinqotho zokubopha. 

    Ababembambile uNsingizi yiwo amadodana kaSifile, ayisithupha, waphelekezelwa emva kwesikhathi eboshelwe esihlahleni !apho, ngamane (amadodana) emusa esiweRi,

njengezwi elaliphume kuSifile lithi, uNxa bemtholile abafana bakhe bangamyisi esiweni esincane kodwa bamyise kwesikhulu ake ayoxhozwaxhozwa inkanyana Ie anayo afe eseke wajulu~a wathi phici; kanti akuzobanjalo njcngoba ethanda; !ntomb, yakhe uqobo, uNomfula, izomfihla pansi kwebhayi Imkh'phe ngembotshana yamagundwane. 

     Umthandazo wakhe, awuthandaz.a kunina, eboshiwe ehlathini, awusho maqedane waxola, kwafika kuye impela uNsingizi ukuba uyara, unina wawuzwa, ngoba wayelokhu cna~e, . epgamlahlanga umntanakhe uNsingizi; noma yena uNsmglzl wayengacabangi ukuba. unina uhamba naye uyamVlkela ezmgoZlIll, ngoba wasewaltbele amazwi kanina amva. lelisa ngawo esehamba cmhlabeni; okuthi uyoba sezinhluphek\~eni inkathi ende, kodwa wogcina ngokujabula. Phela ayeth, noma efika engqondweni yakhe lawomazwi, abuye aweye, awaphikise uNsingizi ethi, "Wayengasho lokhu kuhlupheka, umama, ngoba lokhu akuyikho neze ukuhlupheka, kodwa wukufa." Kufikeengqondweni yakhe ukuba usefile nje kuphela. Noma kunjalo, kodwa wayengakhohlwa ukumthand~za unioa ezinhluphekweni zakhe, ezibika kuyc uNsingizi, unma ukuba am bone lapho ekhona; nempela naye unioa amuzwe, aliphebeze ifu lelo ellmnyama phezu kwakhe. 

     Loy~muntu, ambona ngesithunzi. wamuzwa ngezwi emge,det:t .1:na~ kwakunguye unina kaNsingizi ezomduduza emmlsa ,s,blndl kodwa akwabanjalo, ngoba wahamba ngokumd,klla umna ngokungathembi kwakhe emazwini ayemshiye na:"o; kodwa nokho engamlahlile.      Abathakathi, nxa beya esiweni sabo sokuthakatha babe. ngahambi isishomo funa babonwe, basolwe; kodwa babehamba ngobukhulu ubuchule, ngamunye, ngababili njalo baphike ngokuthi kuyohlanganwa phambili, kungahanjwa ~gandlela mye futhl, kodwa bahambc ngezivundlayo, namadodana abo. zmgangenwa yimithi yabathakathi lapho esiweni, kodwa nokho, zagula emva kwezinsukwana, kubonakala. ukuthl nokho zayithola' kancane imithi yabathakathl zay,hogela.     Umhosha, umfothongwana, lapho kwalimalela khon. uM.hlalhini wawuseduze nje, noma hayi kakhulu, nakwaNdwandwe, nakoSifile, nakwaSibiya ruthi; kanti nakubo kaMahlathini imbala wawuseduze.
